Shenbao Medical and Pharmaceutical Weekly

Introducing the Japanese Trachoma Prevention Association (Continued) 193

— Chen Ren

1. Publication of Association Magazine: Initially four times a year, later (1924) changed to twice a year, with 54 issues published to date. It disseminates essential information on trachoma prevention, achievements in prevention, and association affairs to the public.

2. Holding of Training Seminars: Training seminars are divided into two categories: one for general physicians, to impart trachoma prevention methods, diagnostics, therapeutics, and surgical practice; the other is popular trachoma seminars for the general public, such as schools and hospitality workers, to impart trachoma knowledge for prevention. Each training seminar is organized by local medical associations, other academic societies, or the association itself, with lecturers dispatched by the association to ensure the uniformity of prevention efforts.

3. Publication of "Essentials of Popular Trachoma Knowledge": Tens of thousands of copies are distributed to the public during lectures. "Trachoma Diagnosis, Treatment, Prevention, and Lecture Materials" are also compiled as a reference for general physicians.

4. Utilization of Various Exhibitions: Displaying real objects, wax models of trachoma patients' faces, six types of wax models of trachoma enlarged two times, and other charts related to trachoma transmission and prevention for widespread publicity.

5. Establishment of Free Clinics: Physicians from the association preside over free examinations and treatment for people of all social classes.

6. Production of Trachoma Slide Shows: Despite financial difficulties, the association managed to overcome all obstacles and complete four reels of film, over 3,800 feet in length, about trachoma. It has received high praise from society and recommendations from authorities.

7. Suggestions and Petitions to the Government: As a private group, the association's power is inherently limited. Therefore, prompting government attention and implementing effective trachoma prevention policies are major missions of the association.

(4) Achievements of Japan's Trachoma Prevention Efforts: A brief overview of the achievements of Japan's trachoma prevention efforts is as follows:

1. Mass Screening to Obtain Trachoma Distribution Information: The method is as follows:

A. Complete Examination of All Residents Within a Specific Area: This is unique in the world and amazes all countries.

B. Examination of Various Occupational Groups: Such as nursing staff, barbers, hotel and restaurant staff, etc.

D. Students of All Schools: Including all male and female schools, from elementary to university.

E. Annual Conscription Examinations: Japan implements universal conscription. Every year, draftees are around twenty years old. Great attention is paid to trachoma screening. According to a private report by Professor Ishihara of the Imperial University's ophthalmology department, the statistical report of Japanese conscription examinations is the most accurate and reliable of all Japanese statistical reports because the examiners are all ophthalmology experts.

2. Treatment Facilities and Expenses: Public treatment centers treat an average of 452,000 trachoma patients annually. In addition, there are prefectural treatment centers, privately established clinics, and mobile treatment teams everywhere, giving patients the opportunity to receive treatment, which makes the eradication of trachoma possible.

As for expenses:

Average annual expenses for municipal public clinics: 262,059 yen (an average of 0.60 yen per patient).

Annual average cost of treatment teams in remote areas: approximately 6,192 yen.

Annual average cost of prefectural clinics: 4,726 yen.

Annual average cost of private clinics: 13,088 yen.

Total: 286,065 yen.

3. Results of Prevention Efforts: Here is a report on the trachoma statistics from the Army Ministry's conscription examinations, which are considered precise and reliable:

The trachoma prevalence rate among young men during conscription examinations is as follows:

Taisho Year 1 (1912): 24.0%

Year 4 (1915): 18.0%

Year 7 (1918): 15.3%

Year 10 (1921): 13.9%

Year 13 (1924): 14.5%

Showa Year 2 (1927): 12.7%

Year 5 (1930): 11.1%

Year 8 (1933): 9.6%

It can be seen that trachoma among Japanese youth is decreasing year by year. The achievements of Japan's prevention efforts are generally evident from this. The annual expenditure of about half a million yen is not wasted.

(5) Conclusion:

Having finished my introduction to the Japanese Trachoma Prevention Association, I can't help but feel endless sighs. Japan is a country of the same script and race as us, and in the past, it suffered the exploitation of the great powers along with us. But now, in less than a century, its national power has grown stronger day by day, while our national power has weakened. Japan's restoration was a unified effort, moving forward towards a single ideal. What is this ideal? "To emulate advanced countries and build a modern nation." Today's Japan is the beginning of this ideal. May the people of our country take heed.

Recent Tuberculosis Defense Lines in Various Countries (Continued) 194

— Ding Huikang

Tuberculosis Prevention Guidelines for School Children

The most important aspect of tuberculosis prevention for children is early diagnosis. Children with tuberculosis or suspected of having tuberculosis should be isolated and sent to sanatoriums for treatment. However, it is very difficult to examine children for tuberculosis, and even school doctors cannot do it. Ideally, the tuberculin test is the most appropriate, but if this method cannot be implemented, children with the following conditions should be given special attention by the clinic.

(1) Children with a family history of tuberculosis, especially if their parents, siblings, or sisters had tuberculosis at the time of the child's birth, or died from it.

(2) Children who have tuberculosis in their direct environment.

(3) Children who are very weak and have poor physical development.

(4) Children with lymphatic gland diseases.

(5) Children who are frequently infected with [illegible character] and often drop out of school due to inflammation.

(6) Children with poor appetite.

(7) The recovery period after infectious diseases, especially measles, pertussis, and acute colds.

(8) Children who cough and have fever frequently.

(9) Students or teachers who are found to have open tuberculosis in school. All students in the class or school should be examined.

Tuberculosis Mortality Statistics in Germany in 1931

Compared with the statistics from 1913 to 1928, the tuberculosis mortality statistics in Prussia in 1931 decreased by almost one-third. However, the decrease was not significant in young children aged 2 to 5 and adults aged 25 to 30. School children and those aged 40 to 70 were statistically safer. However, the mortality rate of tuberculosis was extremely high during working ages. The mortality rate among married women did not increase statistically.

Decrease in Tuberculosis Mortality Statistics in the United States

According to Dr. Kellogg's report, the tuberculosis mortality statistics in the United States of America were 204 per 100,000 people in 1904 and only 67 in 1931. This decrease in tuberculosis mortality statistics also has the same tendency in colored people. The reason is that the definite pathological cause has been proven, and especially the progress of surgical methods, the completeness of sanatorium equipment, and the progress of public health. In recent years, the number of tuberculosis deaths has further decreased. For example, in the ten states of the United States, the statistics from January to June 1932 decreased by 8% compared with the same months of the previous year.

Annual Losses Due to Tuberculosis Deaths in France

The annual mortality statistics in France are 690,000 cases, of which 90,000 are due to tuberculosis. Roughly speaking, men account for about 50,000, and women account for about 40,000. The mortality rate of young children under the age of ten has now decreased, but between the ages of ten and twenty, the mortality statistics of both sexes have gradually increased. Afterwards, women gradually decreased to the age of forty, and men decreased to the age of fifty. In France, approximately 300,000 people of working age between the ages of fifteen and fifty-five die from tuberculosis each year, and the impact on the country's productivity is 1.1 billion francs, not to mention the cost of treatment and the subsidies for the families of the deceased. Therefore, the loss is at least 1.5 billion francs per year.

Current Status of Tuberculosis in Norway

52% of Norwegian residents have a positive tuberculin reaction, of which 0.9% are infants under two years old, and 10.99% are children under eighteen years old. All patients with open tuberculosis are called sources of infection (97%), and the patient's residence is called the area of infection (84%). Two-thirds of tuberculosis deaths are caused by infections in their own homes, mostly due to droplet infection. The clinical manifestations of tuberculosis are most likely to occur between the ages of thirteen and thirty, and three-quarters of pleurisy patients mostly occur within three years after infection. Bacterial immunization has a considerable resistance to allergic reactions, but it is ineffective for endogenous disseminated tuberculosis, and congenital resistance is very important. From experience, the only effective way to prevent tuberculosis infection is to isolate the cause of the disease.

Alcohol and Tuberculosis

Observations on the medical records of 1,742 children revealed that the families of more than 50% of children with surgical tuberculosis were drinkers. Since the implementation of prohibition regulations in the Netherlands in 1916, the mortality rate of tuberculosis, especially among elderly male tuberculosis patients, has decreased significantly.

Italian Tuberculosis Prevention Organization

Recently, Italian scholar Molaini published Italy's organization and achievements in tuberculosis prevention at the National Science Conference. Molaini is the dean of the new Carlo Forlani Sanatorium, secretary general of the Italian National Medical Association, and vice president of the National Tuberculosis Prevention Association. His position is extremely important. He said,

Page 16

that since Italy implemented the compulsory insurance law for tuberculosis, the annual tuberculosis mortality statistics have decreased from 50,000 to 40,000 people. Tuberculosis patients should leave their families, and children in the tuberculosis environment are even more important. The important implementation of tuberculosis prevention methods is the compulsory insurance for tuberculosis. All salary levels below 100 Lira per month (1 Lira is equal to 0.20 Chinese yuan) must comply with the tuberculosis insurance law. In addition, the Fascist National Research Institute spares no effort to improve public health and treatment methods. For example, initially tuberculosis patients were only instructed to pay attention to family treatment methods, but now, due to the establishment of a large number of sanatoriums and treatment centers, irregular family treatment methods have been completely abandoned. Molaini believes that sanatoriums should be built on high mountains, and the number of beds should continue to increase. This decrease in tuberculosis mortality statistics is of course not entirely due to direct tuberculosis prevention work, but also due to the improvement of public health. Finally, Molaini also said that physicians who are engaged in tuberculosis prevention work must undergo specialized training, and this kind of work belongs to the country, which will definitely increase the effectiveness of tuberculosis prevention. (Sent from Geneva, Switzerland)

Study on Inoculation (Part 1) 195

— Yue Qi

—Thirteenth Story of Medical Anecdotes—

Anyone familiar with the history of inoculation knows the name Edward Jenner. In medical history, Jenner is revered as the originator of vaccination, and he has always enjoyed the honor of a general medical inventor. In fact, Jenner's honor is somewhat undeserved. What Jenner introduced was the technique of inoculating cowpox to prevent smallpox, but before that, the technique of using human smallpox pus to inoculate the body—the so-called "planting flowers"—had already become popular in Europe. The first person to introduce "planting flowers" to Europe was Lady Mary Wortley Montagu, and its origin was in Turkey.

Lady Montagu was the wife of the British ambassador to Turkey at the time. On April 1, 1717, this ambassador's wife wrote in a letter to a lady in her home country:

"I want to tell you something that I believe will make you want to live here. Smallpox, which is very common and life-threatening in our country, has become completely harmless here due to the invention of Ingrafting. Here, a group of old women make it their specialty to perform this kind of surgery every year in September, when the severe heat has subsided. People ask each other whether their family members are willing to get smallpox once. These people gather together (usually about fifteen or sixteen people), and the old woman comes over, carrying a nutshell of 'top-quality' smallpox pus, and asks you which vein you want her to cut open. You tell her, and she immediately cuts open the skin of that part with a large needle, which will make you feel as if you have been scratched. Then, she puts the smallpox pus from the needle tip into your vein. You will probably start to have a fever on the eighth day. Within a few days, smallpox will appear on your face—no more than twenty or thirty pustules at most. The French ambassador here once joked that the Turks 'eat smallpox' just like other people drink water."

In the half-century after this, there were many famous representatives of the implementation of "planting flowers." Dr. Maitland was Lady Montagu's first British disciple. Princess Caroline persuaded George I to pardon six convicted criminals and have them undergo "planting flowers" as an experiment. Dr. Maitland performed "planting flowers" on these six criminals in 1721. As a result, they all developed mild smallpox and were spared hanging.

In France, King Louis XVI underwent "planting flowers" in 1774. The bold attempt of the royal family was seen as a grand ceremony at the time. Queen's dressmaker Madame Rose Bertin specially created a special headdress in the shape of a smallpox pustule to commemorate this grand ceremony.

In the eighteenth century, the most famous person to perform "planting flowers" was Baron Dimsdale, who was invited by the Russian Queen Catherine II to Russia to perform "planting flowers." At that time, the Russian people not only dared not try "planting flowers," but also regarded Baron Dimsdale as a demon. As soon as they saw him arrive, they ran away. The king specially sent a guard to accompany him to a family to inoculate. The distressed mother curled up in the corner of the house, trying to hide her youngest three-year-old boy. To promote the technique, the King personally underwent the experiment, as did her lover Grigory Orlov and her adopted son Grand Duke Paul. The results of these three were very good, and the trend of planting flowers gradually became popular in the royal family and among the people, and the doctors of St. Petersburg began to learn this surgery.

Talking About My Own Blistering Method for Quitting Smoking 196

— Song Guobin

Origin: My trial use of this method was long before the 8th Far East Tropical Medicine Association. Six years ago, I accidentally read a French magazine and saw an article on using blistering to quit drinking. I was fascinated by it, so I tried using it to quit smoking, and it had a remarkable effect. Later, I taught this method to my classmates at the Aurora University School of Medicine and asked them to practice it in the hospital. As my classmates gradually graduated and spread out in all directions, this method was passed on and gradually became known to the Chinese people. Recently, various drug rehabilitation centers in Shanghai and the entire Longhai Railway have used this method as the only way to quit smoking. The number of smokers who have quit is in the millions. The Ti Ren Hospital, which I and Dr. Yang Yannian run, has used this method to help thousands of people quit smoking over the years, and the results are very impressive. Compared to the tapering method, it is indeed faster and less painful! This method initially used a mixture of ammonia and camphor oil to cause blistering, and those who quit often felt pain. Since switching to domestic cantharidin ointment, there has been no pain at all. Now, because inquiries have been pouring in from all directions, I am writing this to answer them:

Principle: Opium is one of the toxins. Non-addicts who smoke it will be poisoned if they take a slight overdose. Addicts who smoke it will not be harmed even if they take a large dose. Why is this? It is because the human body cannot tolerate foreign substances. When toxins invade, it produces an antitoxin to eliminate them. The same is true for the inhalation of opium. Addicts develop "anti-opium toxins" in their bodies, which neutralize the inhaled opium and create a need. Therefore, the inhaled smoke is eliminated by them, and if they do not smoke for a while, they feel the need. This is why addicts rarely experience poisoning. The fundamental method of quitting smoking is to eliminate these "anti-opium toxins" and restore the body to its pre-addiction state, so that it cannot feel the inhalation of opium, and at the same time, the body has no need for opium. The principle of blistering to quit smoking lies in this. The blister fluid contains this toxin, but once it is extracted and comes into contact with the outside world, it undergoes physical and chemical changes and becomes a special type of allogeneic protein. If this is then injected back into the body of the person trying to quit, it disrupts the blood and throws it off its normal equilibrium state. The "anti-opium toxins" in the body are also precipitated and lose their effect in this chaotic state. This is the so-called "shock" phenomenon. Therefore, after a certain period of time after the injection, those trying to quit not only have no need for opium, but also experience nausea, vomiting, and all kinds of unpleasant allergic reactions if they try to smoke. This is a popular explanation of the principle of blistering to quit smoking.

Precautions for Use: Blistering surgery is well known to doctors and does not need to be described in detail. However, one point that needs to be noted is that the speed of effectiveness is related to the amount of blister fluid. If the amount of fluid produced at one time is more than 10 cc, the effect will be very fast. Otherwise, it must be continued. The amount of blister fluid depends on the thickness of the skin. If the skin is thick, blistering is more difficult and there is less blister fluid. If the skin is tender, blistering is very easy. Do not damage it. Therefore, the length of time for applying the blister varies from person to person. After several experiences, doctors will naturally know this.

Before using this method, those trying to quit may as well smoke opium to their heart's content. They may also smoke after the injection until an allergic reaction occurs, and then the need for opium will disappear.

After blistering, those trying to quit should lie still to avoid damaging the blisters due to movement.

Effect: The effect of the blistering method is not only to quit opium, but also to quit red pills, white powder, morphine, cocaine, and other addictions. According to Dr. Yang Yannian's report, its effectiveness is even faster and more effective than quitting opium.

Smokers who quit using this method not only lose the need for opium, but also develop a kind of aversion to their usual paper cigarettes and alcohol.

However, this aversion is temporary. In other words, the "allergic reaction" disappears after a certain period of time, so there is the possibility of relapse. I have personally seen several people who are weak-willed and come because they are forced by their environment. After quitting, they see that both time and money are saved, and they have no mental or physical pain, so they think about smoking again. When the environment changes, they really re-enter the black list. So they quit and then smoke again, smoke and then quit again, and the cycle continues, repeating as usual. Some people say that this method is too painless and safe, which makes those trying to quit more likely to try it. Is this true? How can it be? This shows that there is a perfect method in the world, but there are also bad people. This is what we hope for the strict enforcement of the smoking ban.

Blistering to quit smoking is very effective, but according to Dr. Yang Yannian's report, it is more difficult to achieve results with smokers who swallow raw opium. Opium contains various toxins, and the degree of poisoning from swallowing it is deeper than from smoking it. In addition, Lin Wenxhong's plaster, which is a variation of raw opium, is also difficult to quit after prolonged use.

Conclusion: In general, when a method is invented, the social criticism is mixed. Some people believe in it, some people oppose it, and some people deliberately slander it. Blistering to quit smoking is the same. I saw in the Kang Le Special Edition of Shen Bao that Mr. Wang Dun'gen's article "Painless Quitting of Smoking" spared no effort to criticize blistering to quit smoking. This really confuses the public and terrifies smokers. Dun'gen's intention was to promote a certain industrial society's egg yolk albumin. I do not want to comment on whether egg yolk albumin is effective, but I cannot correct the inaccuracies in Wang's words! Blistering to quit smoking is the least painful of all quitting methods. In addition to short-term insomnia and leg soreness, there are very few other symptoms. The Black Sea is equal to hell. Leaving the Black Sea is like ascending to heaven from hell. If you cannot even endure these slight aches and pains, how can you be determined to quit?

Common Sense of Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Hygiene 197

— Tang Renjin

(70) Stomatitis (Continued)

(6th) Suppurative Stomatitis

Suppurative stomatitis mostly occurs on the tongue and the floor of the mouth. Therefore, in clinical practice, it can be divided into two types: substantive glossitis and Ludwig's angina. Now, I will talk about them separately.

(A) Substantive Glossitis: This disease in Japan is often caused by insect stings or other minor injuries. However, it can also occur without any cause. Its main symptom is that the patient's tongue is particularly swollen, making it difficult to contain in the mouth. It often protrudes outside the teeth or presses on the throat, causing difficulty breathing. The patient also often feels inconvenienced during talking, chewing, and swallowing. Sometimes, there are also systemic symptoms.

(B) Ludwig's Angina: This disease is actually acute cellulitis of the floor of the mouth. It is generally caused by pyogenic cocci. The source of the inflammation is often in the submandibular gland. This disease has primary and secondary types. However, in clinical practice, it is mostly secondary to diphtheria, scarlet fever, typhoid fever, and influenza. Its main symptoms are redness, swelling, and pain on the skin between the mandibular ramus and the hyoid bone. The floor of the mouth then quickly rises up, and the tongue presses tightly against the palate. Therefore, difficulty can occur during talking, chewing, and swallowing, or it may even be completely impossible. If the disease is severe, it can compress the throat, jugular vein, and esophagus, causing various dangerous symptoms.

This disease mostly develops into an abscess that ruptures outwards or into the oral cavity. It rarely stops the disease process and heals through absorption. Therefore, its prognosis is generally unfavorable. The mortality rate is about 50%. As for its treatment plan, anti-inflammatory methods should be used first. If an abscess has formed, drainage should be performed as soon as possible. This is the key. (End of Stomatitis)

Introducing New Book: Savior of Consumption 198

This book is written by Doctor Guo Renji, clarifying the true nature of consumption (including pulmonary tuberculosis, bone tuberculosis, scrofula, and all kinds of consumption), in intricate detail, and indicating how to prevent and fight consumption, as well as how to conquer the disease of consumption. It is both elegant and popular, can be spoken and acted upon. It is no exaggeration to say that those who suffer from consumption can be taught by reading this book thoroughly. Its contents have been seen scattered in various medical and pharmaceutical supplements, and have long been desired by the general public. It has now been published in a thick hardcover volume, and includes various lung tuberculosis X-ray photographs, copperplates, zinc plates, and many other illustrations. The price is 6 jiao per volume, and an additional 1 jiao 3 fen for postage for out-of-town mail orders. Stamps are accepted at a 10% discount. It is sold at Guo's Social Hygiene Series Editorial Department, No. 40 Yuelai Fang, Caishi Road, French Concession, Shanghai.

A Brief Discussion on Pulmonary Tuberculosis (75) 199

— Hu Jiayan

Lastly, the author has one more thing to declare, which is: the so-called strong will is specifically aimed at the patient's overthinking and anxiety, prescribing the right medicine for the symptom: the indirect purpose is to hope that the patient's body and mind are simultaneously at peace, which will help with other treatments. It is not to say that humans can definitely conquer nature, and that all changes in the condition can be disregarded; that air, nutrition, and various other treatments are superfluous. The extreme of this kind of malpractice is much greater than the former; I hope patients with this disease will understand this clearly.

Section Four: Light Therapy

This is a relatively common treatment method; among them, of course, the most well-known is natural sunlight—it is essential for everyone, and its radiation is undoubtedly beneficial to the human body; the term "sunbathing" has recently been welcomed by the general public. There are also many who advocate the use of sunlight therapy for pulmonary tuberculosis. They believe that patients exposed to sunlight can easily develop skin pigmentation through the power of ultraviolet radiation, resulting in a beneficial impact on the general symptoms of the disease. However, another group of doctors are very skeptical. Because prolonged exposure to sunlight can easily cause bleeding and pleurisy, and many cases of the disease, where the lesions have stopped changing, are rekindled as a result. If you are exposed to sunlight without taking off your clothes, it is easy to cause a state of congestion. Therefore, doctors should be very careful about sunlight therapy; whether it is suitable for the patient, and the determination of the exposure time, are particularly important.

Under what kind of tuberculosis condition is light therapy most suitable? Usually, tuberculosis abscesses, bone tuberculosis, etc., so-called surgical tuberculosis, are mostly suitable. On the pulmonary tuberculosis side, conditions like exudative, early infiltration, cavities, and those with a tendency to cough up blood and pleurisy, should all be avoided. In addition, the hyperplastic sclerotic type can be adopted. Regarding the procedure for exposure, start with the feet, and gradually rise to the head. The head is absolutely unsuitable. The maximum time is thirty minutes at the back; if it is too long, it is extremely easy to cause vomiting and various nervous conditions. Children are sometimes prone to tracheobronchitis, so be careful.

Commentary

Believing Rumors 200

— Ji

Recently, there have been many rumors in this city, so the people who are moving are very active, especially in Zhabei. If you ask how it is not good? Then they say the news is bad, the situation is unstable, and there will be war again. And if you ask who they are fighting with, naturally they will say they are fighting with a certain country.

Is there really going to be war? Is there a possibility of war? Our people have no common sense judgment on this kind of thing, and they most like to listen to rumors, which is extremely pitiful. If you don't believe it, please see that the municipal government has repeatedly denied the rumors and prohibited residents from moving and students from skipping classes, hoping that citizens will use common sense to judge rumors and observe the situation calmly. Also, Mr. He Yingqin, the Minister of Military Administration of our country, said that the central government's policy towards Japan remains unchanged. Anyone with a calm mind and abundant common sense will not be fooled by the rumor-mongers. Although the credibility of newspapers has gone bankrupt, are the municipal government's clear announcements and the Minister of Military Administration's earnest talks also false?

But there are some people who think that what is said in the newspapers is not credible, the municipal government's documents are not credible, and the Minister of Military Administration's talks are not credible, but they only like to listen to a bunch of unfounded rumors, empty words, as if they have evidence and cannot but believe them. What kind of mentality is this? When one family moves, all families follow. When one person spreads the word, everyone agrees. When family A moves, family B will say that family A has moved, and a great disaster is bound to happen, and I cannot but move. When family B moves, families C, D, and others are greatly shocked and say, "Families A and B have moved, and the news must be bad, and we cannot but move." But they don't ask what the facts are. As a result, ordinary people disturb themselves and suffer a loss for nothing.

Investigating the cause of the spread of these rumors, there must be a considerable reason: (1) The market has been sluggish recently, and a group of rogues like to cause trouble so that they can take advantage of the situation and rob. (2) Zhabei suffered very heavy losses since the January 28th Incident and is now a frightened bird. (3) The citizens lack common sense, and once a rumor spreads, they believe it is true, as if disaster is coming. It can be seen from this that the Chinese people do not value reality but only believe in empty words. Therefore, when they hear talk about gods and ghosts, they think about going to sea to seek immortality. When they read martial arts books, they want to go to the mountains to seek Taoism. The Chinese people generally lack scientific common sense and the ability to judge, and they disturb themselves for no reason.

Rubber Plantation 201

— Conglong

I remember that as soon as I stepped out of the door of the elementary school, I always liked to run to my father's rubber plantation, sitting alone under the rubber trees, quietly listening to the gentle warm wind of the southern country whistling a slight whistle, watching the golden dust-like sunlight flickering and tossing on the rubber tree leaves. What made my young mind most happy was Lao Yu, who managed the rubber plantation, who would often give me some delicious food and the bananas that he had planted at the end of the garden himself. Every time he gave me something, his face was always smiling, his mouth cracked open, revealing two rows of black teeth, and he would say, "Fourth Young Master, try it, -- hee hee, it's nothing" -- or "These bananas were just cut from behind the garden, and the taste is not bad."

At the same time, I also liked the cleanliness, neatness, and order of the rubber plantation. Under the rubber trees, it was so neat that almost not even a single weed was allowed to grow, presenting a flat expanse of red. Every day, Lao Yu was always busy wandering around, supervising the workers to pull out the weeds under the trees, with sweat streaming down his back. Sometimes, I really couldn't bear it for him and asked, "Why do you have to pull out the weeds under the trees, Lao Yu?" He quickly turned his head, put on a smiling face, and replied very sincerely: "Fourth Young Master, weeds will take away the fertilizer from the rubber trees, so that the rubber trees cannot grow quickly and produce more rubber juice. -- Hee hee, so the weeds under the trees must be pulled out." When harvesting the rubber juice, groups of Malays, holding parang knives in their hands, would carefully and meticulously cut into the rubber tree trunks. Their cutting method was mostly in the shape of a "V" or a "Y."

My father was very strict in protecting the rubber trees, as if he were protecting his own life. Whenever the price of rubber rose, in order to catch the market, he would harvest it day and night, but my father was always a little worried about working at night, because when the workers were working, they had to hold a lantern in one hand and a parang knife in the other, and sometimes because of their excessive fatigue or insufficient light, they would inevitably damage the tree trunks. Therefore, my father would never easily work at night unless it was absolutely necessary.

There was a time when my father would wear his snowy waist knife after dinner and go to the garden in high spirits. At that time, hearing that my father was going to the rubber plantation always made me feel interested, and I would ask my father to take me with him, but my mother would stop me and say, "What are you doing following along, little kid? Your father is going to hunt down those wildlings who steal rubber seeds." Because at that time, each seed was worth a few cents, and Lao Yu couldn't manage such a large and vast rubber plantation alone at night, so my father had to personally go to the garden every night to help patrol.

Sometimes, after my father had drunk a few cups of burning wine, his face was red, like Guan Gong on the stage, and he was already tipsy. However, at this time, he always liked to open the iron safe and take out the rubber mountain bottom "ya lan" (deed) issued by the government, examining it upside down (naturally, my father didn't recognize the foreign words on it). He would very smugly, like a child, purse his lips and giggle at my mother, saying, "Lan, two hundred 'acres' of rubber mountain; look, -- now each 'acre' is worth more than five hundred yuan."

Once, my father came back from the rubber plantation and put a ball of rubber silk in the iron safe, which made my mother a little curious. She said:

"Why do you even put these rubber silks in the iron safe as if they were treasures?"

But my father replied seriously:

"Don't underestimate these two or three pounds of stuff, they're worth more than ten yuan now." His face showed a smug look.

That could be said to be my father's golden age, and it was also the happiest time in our family, but who could know that that was the most perfect and happiest time!

Now, my father's letters always say that the rubber industry in Nanyang is pitifully depressed, and even if each hundred pounds of rubber is reduced to more than ten yuan, no one will ask about it. Sometimes, because of the family's urgent needs, he is willing to transfer the rubber mountain bottom "ya lan" for three or five yuan per "acre" to others, but no one wants it either.

I returned home last year because I lost my job. When I walked to the rubber plantation that I had been away from for many years, there was not a single person in the rubber plantation. Lao Yu, who managed the rubber plantation, was already gone; it is said that he was dismissed by my father last year. The vast rubber plantation was not managed, and the weeds under the rubber trees grew wildly and vigorously, as high as the shins. No one stole the rubber seeds anymore, and they were allowed to scatter all over the ground, and the small rubber trees grew chaotically.

Recalling the prosperity of my father's rubber plantation in those years, it was only a little over ten years ago, but that prosperity has disappeared like flowing water without a sound!

When I silently recalled the scene of my father with a sharp waist knife inserted between the rubber trees, patrolling back and forth in the rubber plantation in high spirits, and the current desolate and unbearable situation, my heart couldn't help but feel sad.

From then on, I was afraid to go to my father's rubber plantation!

Little Camel Bell Tune 202

— Qin Jian

The days are gradually getting shorter, the summer dusk is now a black night. The clouds in the sky have lost their mixed colors and multifaceted illusions; in the mountain valleys in the wilderness, the maple leaves have gradually faded from their scorching red, and day by day have fallen into the brown days. The sky is gray and dull all day long, and in the low gray sky, it seems to be piled with snow and water. A somewhat cold wind blows threateningly, carrying the breath of yellow sand and dead branches. So, there is a rain in the morning and evening, a chill, and autumn flows past silently like a pile of old shadows, and then the sneaking winter comes, which is very ordinary and without warmth.

Yes, it is already winter. At dusk, sitting alone in the dim light, the surroundings are silent, as indifferent and茫然 as in another world. Looking out from the small window, the sky is such a small and gray-black piece, empty, desolate, and so, images enter a distant and strange realm at this time; I imagine traveling alone in the great desert of Mongolia, the wind rolls up the sand that blinds the eyes, rushing to the endless front, the setting sun spreads melancholy golden light on the boundless earth, between which, a person, a camel, slowly moves inch by inch in this sea of sand. Facing the sunset, it cast a strange shadow on the dry yellow sand; the camel neighed strangely from time to time in the evening wind, and the copper bell tied around its neck emitted an old and depressed sound with its heavy footsteps, sad and mournful, rolled in the brown wind, sparsely, and leisurely spread out, and would never stay on a grain of small sand...

Step by step, walking like that. Hope is lofty, but the current road is so渺茫 and arduous! The night is constantly attacking, and the terrible situation in the early winter desert is unimaginable! Footsteps and heartbeats, everything seems so monotonous! The camel bells scatter into the cold wind one by one, like pearls that have lost their string, like the bells of the underworld.

The setting sun has also disappeared, and the road still cannot be seen to the end; the sea of sand is so wide, and the camel is still swinging its ancient, slow steps, numb and foolishly walking, and so, the sound of copper bells one after another is likely to be imagined as an unfortunate cry for help.

What kind of situation is this? Even the imagination is terrible. However, over the years, I have finally thought of this situation three or four times. That's right, the world is too much like a desert at dusk. And life is like the winter wind! But what about the camel? What about the lonely and tired traveler? What about the camel bells scattered in the north wind?

Carrying heavy and sluggish days, I have lived through the years one by one. People will tremble when they think about it, but let the past go, and what about the future?

The future is a wilderness road without end!

Constantly walking, still so terrifying and lonely; but the sky is gradually darkening, and the wind is gradually becoming fierce. Every moment I can hear the footsteps of these camel-like days, those clear and melancholy camel bells; I feel colder, weaker, and more tired day by day. The sluggish camel bells and the long and desolate journey render life so desolate and terrible that I almost lose the strength to continue walking.

The camel bell rings two sounds, the days slowly climb forward, and in this way, they slowly send people to old age, make people wither, and send people to their final destination.

I saw: in the desolate desert, the camel is carrying the corpses of the previous generation and walking to some place, and the camel bell has become a death knell, constantly striking out some ominous sounds.

The sky in early winter is completely dark, and imagination makes me terrified. I seem to have had another nightmare!

The Seashore of the Island Nation 203

— Xin'er

The dark seawater gradually turns into emerald green, gently shining with beautiful, fine waves. The sea is enveloped in a verdant, fresh and lively appearance. The hearts of weary travelers are filled with bursts of joy.

On the deck, on the ship's railings, the joyful and smiling voices of companions:

"Come out and see, what beautiful mountains and sea..."

It is transmitted into the depressed cabin; so, many smiling faces, yearning for the alien island nation's seashore, gently flutter their hearts open, breathing sweet breaths—a first encounter!

The ship slowly advances along the winding bay of undulating green mountains, gliding over the calm and beautiful sea. Gazing at the iron railings. Lined up beautifully, but very distinctive in their lowliness, the boat and the mountain are so close, people rejoice and reach out, grasping the strangely protruding green mountain that has endured the dangerous winds for several days. Gentle! Without wind and waves, relying on the mountains and forests, infinitely light and clear. Looking back and fondly watching the bay, between the bay and the mountains, small fishing boats, people on the rocks, green trees drooping remotely over the water, leisurely and leisurely low and clever wooden houses. In front, a mountain canyon on both sides has appeared, and the ship rushes towards the canyon: in an instant, the mountain canyon is on the side, and people on the ship can see below the mountain by the water, in the clear and beautiful water, the sand and stones can be counted, and the shadows of fish move faintly. On the mountain tops and between the mountains on both sides, there are also farmland that is high and slanted like steps, and pine forests that seem to be artificially cultivated; there are thick-shaded ancient trunks, and clear and beautiful sparse rows, high and low, and each has its own style.

Sometimes, it suddenly emerges, vast on both sides, and looking forward urgently, the mountains are misty in the distance, on the vast sea, on the blue water without waves, there are dots of fishing boats, and elegant and clever small islands stand alone, which looks like a giant lake. Seeing the ship steadily and strongly sailing towards its destination, at this time I truly feel the high autumn and refreshing air, and the sunlight is particularly gentle. It turns out that the red sun in the sky has become a setting sun. At this time, the ship sails through the green waves, and on both sides, a huge long white ribbon seems to hang down, turning over between the emerald green waters, like a waterfall. Companions point to the black tiles and wooden houses by the mountains near the water in the distance, shouting loudly: That's the swimming beach! A place to escape the summer heat. An island nation has the unique charm of an island nation. I can't help but feel that way!

Germination 204

— Tianshe

The house is very narrow, without even a small courtyard, and the windows are scarce, so you won't know whether it's sunny or rainy outside inside the gate. You can't find a lotus tank or a cymbidium pot in the house, not even a small dish of rock calamus. In such a dark room, where not a trace of sunlight can penetrate, it is indeed not suitable for the survival of plants. People inside are still threatened by an indescribable depression.

But, is this almost an unexpected discovery? I stand by the dilapidated door frame of the kitchen shed, and there is a kind of dazzling life enticing me, I am happy, I even clap my hands and laugh.

Outside the kitchen shed door, there was originally a narrow alley, which a thin body could not pass through. High walls stood on both sides, and broken tiles, garbage, and rotten rags were scattered in a mess, damp and dirty; it was a breeding ground for water rats, earthworms, snails... I hate the smell of that filth, I hate to see that kind of corruption, and I think about moving almost every month. Today, however, I discovered a green bud in this filthy and dark place, about two inches long, as thick as an ear pick, with two small leaves on its head, and white near the roots, fully showing the glory of life. It is not affected by some foul environment, it is like a white navigation mark in the Black Sea. It is growing so courageously in adversity, giving mankind a great inspiration: survival is not limited by the environment.

This bud, this vitality, I silently wish it to grow up quickly, grow up...

But it also makes me worry, that water rat, that earthworm, that snail, that group of unknown dirty insects, will harm the continued growth of this small life, and even devour it. Moreover, the sunlight still does not shine on this alley. Although the germination of plants can be in a dark and humid place, its development and growth always require warm sunlight! So, I will shoulder the mission of protecting life.

This Thing is Too Strange

I think this thing is too strange! I think this thing is too strange! I feel like I've never mistreated you, I feel like I've never offended you, why don't you give me any news? Why don't you tell me your feelings? The green-clothed man comes, the bell rings, I am happy to hear the bell, other people all have letters arriving, but who knows, I have no letters. I look through autumn waves without any news, I stretch my neck and don't see you, tears of hibiscus drip, drip, my heart is full of feelings, I don't know where to start singing.

I think this thing is too strange! I think this thing is too strange! I feel like you were very sincere to me at the beginning, I feel like you were very understanding to me at the beginning, why do you suddenly give me a blow! Why do you suddenly say goodbye to me with difficulty! Recalling when I first met you, you were petite, lively, and very clever, now you have grown up with lofty ambitions, forgetting the past and starting a new opportunity. I left my parents far away for you, I abandoned my hometown far away for you, my liver and intestines are broken inch by inch, my sincere feelings, who knows they will not sink to the bottom of the sea.

Aftersound 209

For the sake of women's health, Fengming Advertising Agency has recently specially invited the famous doctor Mr. Yu Tongfang to write "Women's Hygiene Law". The book is rich in content and has dozens of chapters on effective prescriptions for women's hidden diseases. Women can use this book to pay attention to their usual hygiene when they are not sick. Once a disease strikes, they can refer to "Women's Hygiene Law". Readers who attach a ten-cent stamp can send it to No. 4 Zhengde Lane, Nanchengdu Road, or the fifth floor of the Great World, and the agency will send it.

Regarding the news published in your esteemed publication yesterday that I have left the Shanghai Yan Yan Society and formed another XX Society to broadcast on XHHS. The Shanghai Yan Yan Society was jointly formed by my friends. How could I abandon it halfway? The society did temporarily suspend broadcasting for the sake of strict rectification. The news that I left the society was a misunderstanding by Mr. Xiao Si, which is very strange. Because I still have spare time, I have also joined the Hanyin Society as a violin accompanist and broadcast on XHHS. It is especially important to note that the Hanyin Society was not organized by me. I am sending this letter for correction. Yang Ping

Mr. Yang Zhihong, the violin teacher of the Great Natural Singing Society, participated in the accompaniment at the Qingping Society the day before yesterday. It is said that the Great Natural Singing Society has dissolved invisibly.

Miss Lin Yuwen of the Hanyin Society can play the violin and has studied "Hohmann" by Miki. She is still continuing her studies.

Misses Ying Jian and Ying Lian are both Boy Scouts. The day before yesterday, they were collecting donations on the street for the flood victims in various provinces.

After the Star Light Society stopped broadcasting, Miss Wang Die often performed in various groups. (Above by Xiao Si)

Lianhua Silver News 210

Lianhua's special artistic work "Tianlun," which is eagerly awaited throughout the country, will be premiered this month at Shanghai's largest theater.

"The 'Going to Nature' location shooting team returned from Qingdao and then went to Changhua. The Changhua work lasted four days and has now returned to start shooting interior scenes. The performance time of the play is mostly in summer. Jin Yan, Li Lili, etc., work with bare arms and legs, braving the cold.

Cai Chusheng's new work "The Lost Lamb" boldly confronts reality and handles it with superior techniques. Everything will surpass "Fisherman's Song" and be Cai's proud masterpiece. The whole play is relaxed and funny, but the core is very poignant.

"Hanjiang Luoyan", which took the longest time to film and cost a huge amount of capital, has already captured the great pier scene. This scene took two days and nights to complete. In addition to this scene, a few scattered shots need to be filmed, and the whole play can be completed.

The prop room has recently made thousands of paper lanterns and many paper heads, which are said to be used in the play "Weeping Remnants of Red".

"Lang Taosha" is currently filming a transport ship scene. Jin Yan's sailor outfit shows a calm and powerful performance. Although the ship is placed on land, the background arrangement is ingenious, making it look as if it is sailing on the sea.

There is a movie screening scene in "The Lost Lamb". This movie has a screen and a projector, but the actors' performance is not on the film, but in front of the projector, performing powerful satire, which delights the audience.

In "Three Modern Men", Liu Jiqun sings a new New Fengyang song, as well as "Mama's Song". Han Langan and Yin Xiucen sing a Cuban peanut buying song together.

Ge Zuozhi and Chen Juanjuan play little lovers in the two films "The Lost Lamb" and "慈母曲".

Silver Snippets 211

— Zhi Er

Shi Dongshan's "Song of Everlasting Regret" is currently filming location shots in Hangzhou, staying at the Qintai Second Hotel on West Lake.

It is said that the "Song of Everlasting Regret" location shooting team played two basketball games in Hangzhou, losing to Minsheng Middle School 24 to 32, and winning against Hulin Middle School 30 to 15.

After the Chinese Film Society published an issue of "Ten Days of Film", there has been no news since. It is said that the ocean costs eight yuan, and the person in charge of the association, Xiao Chui, had a big fight with someone named Ding, and Xiao Dun's face was swollen and red, unable to see guests.

The "Resurrection" drama of Diantong is currently rehearsing the first act (a total of five acts). It is planned to rehearse each act for six days, completing the rehearsal within a month, from 2:00 PM to 8:00 PM every day.

The outside world is rumored that the female lead of "Resurrection" is Lan Ping. After investigation, this is not accurate. The female lead is actually Miss Chen Boer. As for Lan Ping, there is no role for her in "Resurrection".

Tian Han Writes Songs 212

Mr. Tian Han's literary and academic achievements and thoughts are admired by everyone. He can write the sad and complex life in novels, and he can also write the sad and complex life in songs, and he can make readers, singers, and listeners be moved.

The songs in "Heroes of the Times" were written by Mr. Tian Han. They were the first songs he wrote after living in Nanjing for a long time. He wrote all the phenomena of the play in these songs. He wrote all the indignation of the play in these songs. The tragic singing can especially arouse magnificent feelings, like a lion's roar, like a tiger's roar, making listeners not know whether it is a song - a twilight drum, a morning bell!
